 inamen jamnagar main township bananaa, samgr offis campus, rilanyas retail ke kanjumar point kaa dizin taiyaar karnaa vagairah hai

 saamaajik jimmedaari ke tahat is foundation ne pichley saal 712 karod rupye kharch kiye the

 unhone kaha ki reliance industries kaa lakshya lakhon logon kii jindagi main khushiyaan laana he
 Though company sources said that this is a natural process but critics say that this has been done due to the new company law which makes it mandatory to have at least one female director on the board
 rafel kaa maamla khatm hone kaa naam hi nahin le rahaa he
 Everyday some such statements come which do not let the matter be suppressed
 
 The latest statement is by former French President Hollande
 
 In which he said that the Indian government had suggested the name of Anil Ambani's Reliance Group as a partner, after which the French company Dassault had no option left
 
 This is a statement that is nothing short of a lifeline for the Congress in India
 
 Hollande was the President of France when the deal took place
 
 Hollande was the President of France from 2012 to 2017 while the Rafale deal was signed in 2016
 
 Hollande said this to a French website
 
 This interview is on the French website, but only those who have paid the fees of this website can read it
 
 But important parts of this interview have been tweeted by many French journalists
 
 
 ek patrkaar ne twit kar ke kaha he ki oland ne kaha he ki hamaare paas koi vikalp nahin tha
 
 hamen jo vaartakar diya gaya hamane usee se baatcheet shuru kar di

e

 congress ne sivisi yani satarkta ayog se sabhi kagajaat jabt karne or exiaar karne kii maang kii he

 kuch sawaal hai jo ve lagaataar puch rahe hai sarkaar se

 1

 iske liye sharir ko nutrients kii jarurat padati he

 iske alaava khaali pet sone se cholesterol or thyroid level bhi bigadataa he

 mukhya sachiv dwaara jari kiye gaye disha nirdesh ke anusaar pradhan sachiv, kamishnar, jiladhikari, cirkil adhikari or prakhand vikaas padaadhikari, in sabhi ko har shuukravaar ko apane offis main aam aadmi se milane or unki samasyaon ko sunne ke liye nirdeshit kiya gaya he

 in sabhi sarkari babu ko yah bhi disha nirdesh jari kiya gaya he ki yah sabhi apni upasthiti apane daftar yaa phir jila mukhyalay main prayek somvaar, mangalvaar or shuukravaar ko sunishchit karen or baaki ke dinon main vah apane apane kshetra kaa daura karen
 These government babus have been ordered to take stock of the development works related to their respective departments while visiting the area

 One of the films released this Friday is Anurag Kashyap's Raman Raghav 2
 0', jisamen mukhya bhoomikaayen nibhaai hai navazuddin siddiki, vicky kaushal, amrutha subhash or shobhita dhulipala ne
 The film has been written by Anurag and Vasan Bala
 produs kiya he phentom films ne
 Raman Raghav is a film based on the '60s serial killer
 yah bataanaa zaruri he ki film raman raghav kii jeevani nahin he
 Serial killer inspired film, then of course, the film will also have murders one after the other, and there is no revenge behind these killings, only the craze
 film main duusari ore he ek police afasar, jiske qirdaar main hai vicky kaushal, jinke khud ke kai negative shades hai
 In the film's story, as the police come out to catch the culprit, it becomes clear that director Anurag Kashyap is also comparing a criminal and a police officer
 yani film main bataaya jaataa he ki donon qirdaaron main zyaada fark nahin he sivaay vardi ke
 
 
 So this was just a glimpse of the film's story
 
 
 ab baat karte hai film kii kaamiyon or kuubiyon kii
 The film takes a lot of time to convey Raman, i
e
 Nawaz's stalker and his thinking to the audience, and the unproven murders one after the other does not cause any stir in the mind or mind of the audience
 ek serial killer ke paas na rahane ko jagah he, na khaane kaa intazaam, lekin uski is haalat par darshakon ko dayaa aani mushkil he

 haa, interval ke baad kahani kaa rukh zaraa badla-sa laga
 Understood what the director is pointing to
 yani police afasar or ek apradhi kii tulana, haalanki isamen bhi kuch nayaapan nahin laga
 'badlapur' was also trying to say this to some extent
 
 
 drugs, police afasar kii garlfriend or unka rishta, kaanoon kaa rakhwala hi gaiyrkanoonee kaamon main lipt jaise kuch utaar-chadhaav
 
 
 But overall this story and screenplay can prove to be unsuccessful in maintaining the viewer's interest
 kuubiyon kii baat karen to film kii cinemetographi acchhee he
 Ram Sampath's music is good, which empowers the film's narrator
 vicky kaushal kii acting acchhee he, lekin unke qirdaar ko or sateek banane kii zarurat thi
 The comments nawaz film main thik hai, par mushkil yah he ki vah khud ko baar-baar ek jaisaa dikhaa rahe hai

 unhen khud ko dohraane se bachanaa chahie

 Now let's talk about the shortcomings and weaknesses of the film
 film main raman, yani nawaz ke qirdaar or uski soch ko darshakon tak pahunchane main film bahut samay le leti he or ek ke baad ek bina kaaran ho rahi hatyaein darshakon ke man yaa dimag main koi halchal paidaa nahin karatin
 a serial killer has no place to live, no food, but it is difficult for the audience to take pity on his condition
 film main jhakzorne vaale lamhe ke intazaar main interval aa jaataa he
 Yes, the story changed a bit after the interval
 samaj aayaa ki nirdeshak kis ore ishaara kar rahe hai
 That is, the comparison of a police officer and a criminal, although there was nothing new in this
 'badlapur' bhi kuch had tak yahi kehane kii koshish kar rahi thi
 
 
 Some ups and downs like drugs, police officer's girlfriends and their relationship, the law keeper is involved in illegal activities
 
 
 par kul milakar yah kahani or screenple darshakon kii ruchi banaae rakhane main naakaam sabit ho sakate hai
 Talking about the features, the cinematography of the film is good
 ram sampath kaa sangeet acha he, jo film ke nerrative ko shashakt karata he
 Vicky Kaushal's acting is good, but his tenor needed to be more precise
 tippaniyan Nawaz is fine in the film, but the difficulty is that he is showing himself the same again and again
 'badlapur' or 'kik' jaisi filmon main bhi unhone vahi kiya tha, jo yahaan karte dikhe
 They should avoid repeating themselves
 or aakiri achchhai film kii he iskaa climex
 By the way, remember, the climax was better than the whole film, not new or different
